Stopped here on the way to a show at the Fox Theater. I noticed they offered a whole menu of martinis, so I ordered a gin martini. I don't know what I was served, but it was not what I ordered. I'm not even sure it was gin. I couldn't pinpoint the flavor. About 15 minutes after I ordered, I was served some kind of liquid in a margarita glass, with lime wedges. I could not finish the drink it was so terrible.

Bathroom requires obtaining a giant key from the staff, and when I was there, they seemed understaffed, so it took a while.

On the upside, the food was tasty with generous sizes.< /review>

< Text>
This is copied from my Yelp review in August 2019 when the work was originally done. I feel the same way today. Everything has held up beautifully!

I don't know what we're more pleased with: Our gorgeous garage floor, our beautiful cabinets, or the A+ service from every individual we had with OGS. I'm a property manager of 30+ years, with high standards, and the quality of work and courteous, professional people exceeded my expectations. Everyone with whom I've dealt (from owner to each worker) has been courteous, reliable, helpful, patient, and more.

The flooring makes the garage look like an interior room - gorgeous! It is bright and smooth, with just enough roughness to help prevent slips. And it's going to be so easy to keep clean. Dustin and Hector took extra care in its installation; e.g., extra concrete prep for cracks, taping off the kitchen door so no dust came inside, and more. When they left, other than the floor, there was nothing to know they had been there - spotless.

The cabinets were made to exact measurement requirements, the material is strong and feels substantial. The hinges and drawers function smoothly. Varand and Victor were perfectionists in their installation, ensuring every piece was perfectly level, secure, and no screw was exposed (even ones against a wall that would never be seen). It ended up I had a gas valve in the way that I didn't think was where it was, and they kindly discussed options and worked extra to accommodate the pipe. They, too, left the garage and new cabinets spotless.

Jay worked with me on the order, and I admit (a bit embarrassingly), I changed my mind on cabinet measurements a few times. Jay was patient making the changes in the drawings and pricing and showed nothing but patience with me.

Now, pulling into our garage makes me smile, as it's like an extra room in our home - a very nice extra room!<//Text>

Good food, affordable, nice portions, welcoming and relaxed atmosphere. The chicken fried steak was insanely tender and juicy, and the Tijuana Scrambled was a great combination of flavors. <user>114740554833993176464</user><Name>Joseph Kimbrell</Name><date>1567411746327< /date><Rate>3</Rate>< Review>
Well...it was quite an experience to try this place. First impression not good, entering one of the waitresses told me that considering it was just me, I should be seated at the counter, because they were extremely busy, so I did precisely that.
After 10 minutes seated and looking how waitresses and busboys passed by without even looking at me, call the attention of 1 of the waitress and she finally gave me a menu.
Decided just to have a malt and an appetizer, considering that supposedly they were extremely busy, glad I did just that, because for my small order it took them 20 more minutes to just give me the appetizer I order and apologies from the waitress, because she couldn't prepare my malt, instead she gave me ice tea for the inconvenience.
After I finished my appetizer, she finally got time to prepare my malt, but not the one I ordered previously, but just a vanilla one, when I ordered butterscotch, so quite a different flavor.
Finally noticed that there was a very nice couple that arrived about 10 minutes after I did at the end of the counter, who were still waiting for their food when I was leaving, so that gave me the correct impression, that or they are lacking personnel or definitely there's a bigger problem between the service and the kitchen, to create such an awful delay like this, between orders.
Definitely and quite sure, I won't be back at least for quite awhile or until I heard better reviews from someone else!!!</Review>

Once she finally got around to taking our order, it went well. We were served our main plates, then we had to flag down the waitress for anything & everything after that & EVERY SINGLE THING, from missing silverware to coffee & water refills, creamer, sugar, jelly, ranch dressing, etc..... were plopped on the edge of the table as she walked past. VERY  UNPROFESSIONAL!!!!

We are not needy customers, but we do expect proper restaraunt service to go along with our meal (& we tip accordingly). Isn't that half the point of going out to eat?
